ü£ PHASE 3 ü\ DETAILED DESIGN: BOOKING SAGA

3.1 Saga Orchestration Flow ü\ Full State Machine + Compensations

T?ng quan lu?ng Happy Path & Compensation:

stateDiagram-v2                                                                                                                                                                                                         
[*] --> INITIATED : POST /bookings

      INITIATED --> SEATS_HELD : HoldSeats() OK
      INITIATED --> FAILED : HoldSeats() FAILED\n(seats unavailable)                                                                                                                                                      
                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
      SEATS_HELD --> VOUCHER_APPLIED : ValidateVoucher() OK
      SEATS_HELD --> PAYMENT_PENDING : No voucher                                                                                                                                                                         
      SEATS_HELD --> COMPENSATING : ValidateVoucher() FAILED                                                                                                                                                              
      VOUCHER_APPLIED --> PAYMENT_PENDING : InitiatePayment() OK                                                                                                                                                          
      VOUCHER_APPLIED --> COMPENSATING : InitiatePayment() FAILED                                                                                                                                                         
                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
      PAYMENT_PENDING --> CONFIRMING : PaymentCompleted event
      PAYMENT_PENDING --> COMPENSATING : PaymentFailed event                                                                                                                                                              
      PAYMENT_PENDING --> COMPENSATING : 10min TTL expired                                                                                                                                                                
   
      CONFIRMING --> CONFIRMED : ConfirmSeats() OK\n+ RedeemVoucher() OK                                                                                                                                                  
      CONFIRMING --> COMPENSATING : ConfirmSeats() FAILED\n(rare ü\ seats already held)
                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
      CONFIRMED --> [*] : BookingConfirmed published\nDownstream: Ticket + Notification                                                                                                                                   
                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
      COMPENSATING --> CANCELLED : All compensations done\nSeatsReleased + VoucherVoided\n+ RefundInitiated (if paid)                                                                                                     
                  
      CANCELLED --> [*]                                                                                                                                                                                                   
      FAILED --> [*]
                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
      note right of PAYMENT_PENDING
          Redis TTL = 600s (10 ph?t)
          Quartz job poll m?i 30s                                                                                                                                                                                         
          check expired bookings
      end note                                                                                                                                                                                                            
                  
      note right of COMPENSATING                                                                                                                                                                                          
          Compensation l? sequential:
          1. RefundPayment (n?u ?? thanh to?n)                                                                                                                                                                            
          2. ReleaseSeats
          3. VoidVoucher (n?u ?? redeem)                                                                                                                                                                                  
      end note    

Chi ti?t t?ng b??c + Compensation:

flowchart TD                                                                                                                                                                                                            
START([User g?i POST /bookings]) --> S0

      S0["Step 0: Create Booking\nü\ü\ü\ü\ü\ü\ü\ü\ü\\n? T?o Booking aggregate\n? status = INITIATED\n? correlationId = UUID\n? Write to booking_db\n? Write to outbox table\n? Return 202 Accepted + bookingId"]                   
                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
      S0 --> S1                                                                                                                                                                                                           
                  
      S1{"Step 1: Hold Seats\ngRPC ü© showtime-service\nü\ü\ü\ü\ü\ü\ü\ü\ü\\nHoldSeats(showtimeId, seatIds[],\nbookingId, ttl=600s)"}                                                                                                
   
      S1 -->|SUCCESS| S1_OK["Redis: HSET seat:showtime:seatId\n= HELD, bookingId, expiresAt\nBooking: status = SEATS_HELD"]                                                                                               
      S1 -->|SEATS_TAKEN| C1["? Compensation C1\nBooking: status = FAILED\nReason: SEATS_UNAVAILABLE\nü© Kh?ng c?n release\nü© Publish BookingFailed event"]
                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
      S1_OK --> S2                                                                                                                                                                                                        
                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
      S2{"Step 2: Validate Voucher\ngRPC ü© promotion-service\n[OPTIONAL ü\ n?u c? voucher]\nü\ü\ü\ü\ü\ü\ü\ü\ü\\nValidateVoucher(code, userId,\ntotalAmount)"}                                                                       
                  
      S2 -->|VALID| S2_OK["discountAmount applied\nBooking: status = VOUCHER_APPLIED\nfinalAmount calculated"]                                                                                                            
      S2 -->|INVALID/EXPIRED| C2["? Compensation C2\n1. ReleaseSeats() gRPC\n   showtime: HELDü©AVAILABLE\n2. Booking: status = FAILED\nReason: INVALID_VOUCHER"]
      S2 -->|NO_VOUCHER| S3                                                                                                                                                                                               
                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
      S2_OK --> S3                                                                                                                                                                                                        
                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
      S3{"Step 3: Initiate Payment\ngRPC ü© payment-service\nü\ü\ü\ü\ü\ü\ü\ü\ü\\nInitiatePayment(bookingId,\namount, method, userId)"}                                                                                              
   
      S3 -->|SUCCESS| S3_OK["Payment record: PENDING\npaymentUrl returned\nBooking: status = PAYMENT_PENDING\nQuartz job scheduled: T+600s"]                                                                              
      S3 -->|PSP_ERROR| C3["? Compensation C3\n1. ReleaseSeats() gRPC\n2. VoidVoucher() [if applied]\n3. Booking: status = FAILED\nReason: PAYMENT_INIT_FAILED"]
                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
      S3_OK --> WAIT_PAY
                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
      WAIT_PAY(["? Waiting for Payment...\nUser on PSP page\nTTL countdown: 10 min"])                                                                                                                                    ä¤
   
      WAIT_PAY -->|"PaymentCompleted\n(RabbitMQ event)"| S4                                                                                                                                                               
      WAIT_PAY -->|"PaymentFailed\n(RabbitMQ event)"| C4A
      WAIT_PAY -->|"TTL Expired\n(Quartz job)"| C4B                                                                                                                                                                       
                  
      C4A["? Compensation C4A\n1. Booking: status=COMPENSATING\n2. ReleaseSeats() gRPC\n3. VoidVoucher() [if applied]\n4. Booking: status=CANCELLED\nReason: PAYMENT_FAILED"]                                            ä¤
                  
      C4B["? Compensation C4B\n1. Booking: status=COMPENSATING\n2. CancelPayment() gRPC\n3. ReleaseSeats() gRPC\n4. VoidVoucher() [if applied]\n5. Booking: status=CANCELLED\nReason: PAYMENT_TIMEOUT"]                  ä¤
                  
      S4{"Step 4: Confirm Seats\ngRPC ü© showtime-service\nü\ü\ü\ü\ü\ü\ü\ü\ü\\nConfirmSeats(showtimeId,\nseatIds[], bookingId)"}                                                                                                    
                  
      S4 -->|SUCCESS| S5                                                                                                                                                                                                  
      S4 -->|FAILED| C5["? Compensation C5 (RARE)\nSeats ?? HELD b?i m?nh\nn?n ConfirmSeats g?n nh? kh?ng fail\nN?u fail: Refund + Release\nBooking: CANCELLED"]
                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
      S5{"Step 5: Redeem Voucher\ngRPC ü© promotion-service\n[if voucher was applied]\nü\ü\ü\ü\ü\ü\ü\ü\ü\\nRedeemVoucher(code, bookingId)"}                                                                                         
                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
      S5 -->|SUCCESS| S6                                                                                                                                                                                                  
      S5 -->|FAILED| C5

      S6["Step 6: Finalize\nü\ü\ü\ü\ü\ü\ü\ü\ü\\n? Booking: status = CONFIRMED\n? Write BookingConfirmed to outbox\n? Debezium picks up ü© RabbitMQ\n? Downstream async:\n  ü© ticket-service (issue QR)\n  ü© notification-service    
(email+push)"]

      S6 --> END([? Booking Complete])                                                                                                                                                                                   ä¤
