? AggregateRoot.java ü\ Shared Base Class (cinetix-common lib):

// libs/cinetix-common/.../domain/AggregateRoot.java
package com.cinetix.common.domain;

import jakarta.persistence.MappedSuperclass;
import jakarta.persistence.Transient;                                                                                                                                                                                   
import java.util.*;

@MappedSuperclass                                                                                                                                                                                                       
public abstract class AggregateRoot<ID> {

      @Transient
      private final List<DomainEvent> domainEvents = new ArrayList<>();
                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
      public abstract ID getId();
                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
      protected void registerEvent(DomainEvent event) {                                                                                                                                                                   
          Objects.requireNonNull(event, "Domain event cannot be null");
          domainEvents.add(event);                                                                                                                                                                                        
      }                                                                                                                                                                                                                   
   
      /**                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
       * Pull events v? clear buffer.
       * G?i sau khi save aggregate ?? tr?nh duplicate publish.
       */                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
      public List<DomainEvent> pullDomainEvents() {
          var copy = List.copyOf(domainEvents);                                                                                                                                                                           
          domainEvents.clear();                                                                                                                                                                                           
          return copy;
      }                                                                                                                                                                                                                   
                  
      public boolean hasDomainEvents() {
          return !domainEvents.isEmpty();
      }                                                                                                                                                                                                                   
}

// ä¤ä¤ DomainEvent interface ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤                                                                                                                                       
public interface DomainEvent {
UUID getEventId();                                                                                                                                                                                                  
String getEventType();       // "booking.events.confirmed.v1"
String getAggregateType();   // "Booking"                                                                                                                                                                           
Object getAggregateId();     // BookingId
Instant getOccurredAt();                                                                                                                                                                                            
String getVersion();         // "v1"
}

// ä¤ä¤ BookingConfirmedEvent example ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤                                                                                                                                       
public record BookingConfirmedEvent(
UUID     eventId,                                                                                                                                                                                                   
BookingId aggregateId,
CustomerId customerId,                                                                                                                                                                                              
ShowtimeId showtimeId,
List<SeatId> seatIds,                                                                                                                                                                                               
Money    finalAmount,
VoucherCode voucher,                                                                                                                                                                                                
Instant  confirmedAt
) implements DomainEvent {

      public static BookingConfirmedEvent from(Booking booking, Instant at) {                                                                                                                                             
          return new BookingConfirmedEvent(
              UUID.randomUUID(),                                                                                                                                                                                          
              booking.getId(),
              booking.getCustomerId(),
              booking.getShowtimeId(),
              booking.getSeatIds(),                                                                                                                                                                                       
              booking.getFinalAmount(),
              booking.getAppliedVoucher(),                                                                                                                                                                                
              at  
          );
      }

      @Override public UUID    getEventId()       { return eventId; }                                                                                                                                                     
      @Override public String  getEventType()     { return "booking.events.confirmed.v1"; }
      @Override public String  getAggregateType() { return "Booking"; }                                                                                                                                                   
      @Override public Object  getAggregateId()   { return aggregateId; }                                                                                                                                                 
      @Override public Instant getOccurredAt()    { return confirmedAt; }
      @Override public String  getVersion()       { return "v1"; }                                                                                                                                                        
}
   
---                                                                                                                                                                                                                     
? Spring Modulith ü\ Enforce Module Boundaries:

// booking-service/src/test/java/com/cinetix/booking/ModularityTest.java
package com.cinetix.booking;

import org.junit.jupiter.api.Test;                                                                                                                                                                                      
import org.springframework.modulith.core.ApplicationModules;
import org.springframework.modulith.docs.Documenter;

class ModularityTest {

      // ApplicationModules detect modules b?ng package structure                                                                                                                                                         
      static ApplicationModules modules =
          ApplicationModules.of(BookingServiceApplication.class);                                                                                                                                                         
                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
      @Test
      void verifyModuleStructure() {                                                                                                                                                                                      
          // Fail n?u c? circular dependency ho?c module access violation
          modules.verify();                                                                                                                                                                                               
      }
                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
      @Test       
      void generateDocumentation() {
          new Documenter(modules)
              .writeModulesAsPlantUml()                                                                                                                                                                                   
              .writeIndividualModulesAsPlantUml();
      }                                                                                                                                                                                                                   
}

// K?t qu?: Spring Modulith s? c?nh b?o n?u:                                                                                                                                                                            
// - domain/ import t? infrastructure/ (KH?NG ???c)
// - application/ import tr?c ti?p JPA entities (KH?NG ???c ü\ ph?i qua port)                                                                                                                                            
// - 2 modules import l?n nhau (circular dependency)

7.1 Dockerfile ü\ Multi-Stage Build

GraalVM Native Image ü\ C? n?n d?ng kh?ng?

äĪä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä”ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä”ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤äó                                                                                                                                           
äĀ                     äĀ JVM Layered JAR (JRE 21) äĀ GraalVM Native Image     äĀ
äźä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä®ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä®ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¦                                                                                                                                           
äĀ Startup time        äĀ 3-8 gi?y                 äĀ 50-200ms ?              äĀ
äĀ Memory usage        äĀ 256-512MB                äĀ 64-128MB ?              äĀ                                                                                                                                           ä¤
äĀ Build time CI       äĀ 2-3 ph?t ?              äĀ 8-15 ph?t  ??             äĀ
äĀ Debug/profiling     äĀ Full JVM tools ?         äĀ Limited  ??               äĀ                                                                                                                                          
äĀ Reflection/dynamic  äĀ Full support ?           äĀ C?n hints file  ??        äĀ                                                                                                                                          
äĀ Spring Boot support äĀ Excellent ?              äĀ Good (3.x+) ?           äĀ                                                                                                                                            
äĀ Testcontainers      äĀ ? Easy                   äĀ  ?? Complex               äĀ                                                                                                                                          
äĀ JPA / Hibernate     äĀ ? Perfect                äĀ  ?? C?n c?u h?nh th?m    äĀ                                                                                                                                           
äĀ gRPC                äĀ ?                        äĀ ä¤?? Protobuf reflection   äĀ                                                                                                                                          
äżä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä©ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä©ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤äŻ

Khuy?n ngh?: JVM Layered JAR cho MVP v? production hi?n t?i.                                                                                                                                                            
L? do: booking-service d?ng nhi?u reflection (JPA, Jackson, gRPC protobuf),                                                                                                                                             
GraalVM c?n hints ph?c t?p. Startup time 5s v?i K8s readiness probe                                                                                                                                              
l? ho?n to?n ch?p nh?n ???c. Revisit khi h? th?ng stable.

Dockerfile ü\ Production-Optimized:

# ???????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????
# Stage 1: Build
# ???????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????
FROM eclipse-temurin:21-jdk-alpine AS builder

WORKDIR /workspace

# Cache Maven dependencies ri?ng (layer n?y ch? rebuild khi pom.xml thay ??i)
COPY .mvn/ .mvn/
COPY mvnw pom.xml ./                                                                                                                                                                                                    
COPY libs/cinetix-common/pom.xml       libs/cinetix-common/
COPY libs/cinetix-security/pom.xml     libs/cinetix-security/                                                                                                                                                           
COPY libs/cinetix-outbox/pom.xml       libs/cinetix-outbox/
COPY libs/cinetix-grpc-stubs/pom.xml   libs/cinetix-grpc-stubs/                                                                                                                                                         
COPY services/booking-service/pom.xml  services/booking-service/

# Download dependencies (cached n?u pom kh?ng ??i)
RUN ./mvnw dependency:go-offline -pl services/booking-service \                                                                                                                                                         
-am -q --no-transfer-progress

# Copy source v? build
COPY libs/             libs/                                                                                                                                                                                            
COPY services/booking-service/ services/booking-service/
COPY proto/            proto/

RUN ./mvnw package -pl services/booking-service \                                                                                                                                                                       
-am -DskipTests --no-transfer-progress -q

# Extract layered JAR (Spring Boot layered jar feature)
RUN java -Djarmode=layertools \
-jar services/booking-service/target/booking-service-*.jar \                                                                                                                                                        
extract --destination /workspace/extracted

# ???????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????
# Stage 2: Runtime ü\ minimal JRE image
# ???????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????
FROM eclipse-temurin:21-jre-alpine AS runtime

# Security: ch?y v?i non-root user
RUN addgroup -S appgroup && adduser -S appuser -G appgroup                                                                                                                                                              
USER appuser

WORKDIR /app

# Copy layers theo th? t? ?t thay ??i ü© nhi?u thay ??i nh?t
# Docker cache s? reuse layers kh?ng ??i
COPY --from=builder --chown=appuser:appgroup \                                                                                                                                                                          
/workspace/extracted/dependencies/          ./                                                                                                                                                                      
COPY --from=builder --chown=appuser:appgroup \                                                                                                                                                                          
/workspace/extracted/spring-boot-loader/    ./                                                                                                                                                                      
COPY --from=builder --chown=appuser:appgroup \                                                                                                                                                                          
/workspace/extracted/snapshot-dependencies/ ./
COPY --from=builder --chown=appuser:appgroup \                                                                                                                                                                          
/workspace/extracted/application/           ./

# Health check (K8s c?ng t? check nh?ng docker-compose c?n)
HEALTHCHECK --interval=30s --timeout=5s --start-period=60s --retries=3 \
CMD wget -qO- http://localhost:8082/actuator/health || exit 1

EXPOSE 8082 9082

# JVM flags t?i ?u cho container
ENTRYPOINT ["java", \
"-XX:+UseContainerSupport", \                                                                                                                                                                                       
"-XX:MaxRAMPercentage=75.0", \
"-XX:InitialRAMPercentage=50.0", \
"-XX:+OptimizeStringConcat", \                                                                                                                                                                                      
"-XX:+UseG1GC", \
"-XX:MaxGCPauseMillis=200", \                                                                                                                                                                                       
"-Djava.security.egd=file:/dev/./urandom", \
"-Dspring.profiles.active=${SPRING_PROFILES_ACTIVE:docker}", \                                                                                                                                                      
"org.springframework.boot.loader.launch.JarLauncher"]

7.2 docker-compose.yml ü\ Full Dev Local Stack

# infrastructure/docker/docker-compose.yml
version: "3.9"

# ä¤ä¤ä¤ Networks ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤
networks:                                                                                                                                                                                                               
cinetix-net:                                                                                                                                                                                                          
driver: bridge
ipam:                                                                                                                                                                                                               
config:   
- subnet: 172.20.0.0/16

# ä¤ä¤ä¤ Volumes ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤
volumes:
postgres_identity:   {}                                                                                                                                                                                               
postgres_movie:      {}
postgres_cinema:     {}
postgres_showtime:   {}
postgres_booking:    {}
postgres_payment:    {}                                                                                                                                                                                               
postgres_ticket:     {}
postgres_promotion:  {}                                                                                                                                                                                               
postgres_notif:      {}
postgres_chat:       {}
postgres_keycloak:   {}                                                                                                                                                                                               
redis_data:          {}
rabbitmq_data:       {}                                                                                                                                                                                               
minio_data:          {}

# ???????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????
# INFRASTRUCTURE SERVICES
# ???????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????
services:

    # ä¤ä¤ PostgreSQL instances (1 per service) ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤                                                                                                                                        
    # Dev: d?ng chung 1 Postgres instance, m?i service 1 database ri?ng
    # Production: m?i service 1 Postgres instance ri?ng tr?n K8s                                                                                                                                                          
    postgres:                                                                                                                                                                                                             
      image: postgres:16-alpine                                                                                                                                                                                           
      container_name: cinetix-postgres                                                                                                                                                                                    
      environment:
        POSTGRES_USER:     postgres
        POSTGRES_PASSWORD: postgres                                                                                                                                                                                       
        POSTGRES_MULTIPLE_DATABASES: >
          identity_db,movie_db,cinema_db,showtime_db,                                                                                                                                                                     
          booking_db,payment_db,ticket_db,promotion_db,                                                                                                                                                                   
          notif_db,chat_db,keycloak_db
      volumes:                                                                                                                                                                                                            
        - postgres_booking:/var/lib/postgresql/data
        - ./init-scripts/create-databases.sh:/docker-entrypoint-initdb.d/init.sh                                                                                                                                          
      ports:                                                                                                                                                                                                              
        - "5432:5432"                                                                                                                                                                                                     
      networks:                                                                                                                                                                                                           
        - cinetix-net
      healthcheck:
        test: ["CMD-SHELL", "pg_isready -U postgres"]
        interval: 10s                                                                                                                                                                                                     
        timeout: 5s
        retries: 5                                                                                                                                                                                                        
                  
    # ä¤ä¤ Redis ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤
    redis:
      image: redis:7-alpine
      container_name: cinetix-redis                                                                                                                                                                                       
      command: >
        redis-server                                                                                                                                                                                                      
        --requirepass redis_secret
        --appendonly yes
        --maxmemory 512mb
        --maxmemory-policy allkeys-lru                                                                                                                                                                                    
      volumes:
        - redis_data:/data                                                                                                                                                                                                
      ports:      
        - "6379:6379"
      networks:
        - cinetix-net
      healthcheck:
        test: ["CMD", "redis-cli", "-a", "redis_secret", "ping"]                                                                                                                                                          
        interval: 10s
        timeout: 3s                                                                                                                                                                                                       
        retries: 5

    # ä¤ä¤ RabbitMQ ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤                                                                                                                                       
    rabbitmq:
      image: rabbitmq:3.13-management-alpine                                                                                                                                                                              
      container_name: cinetix-rabbitmq
      environment:
        RABBITMQ_DEFAULT_USER: cinetix                                                                                                                                                                                    
        RABBITMQ_DEFAULT_PASS: cinetix_secret
        RABBITMQ_DEFAULT_VHOST: /cinetix                                                                                                                                                                                  
      volumes:                                                                                                                                                                                                            
        - rabbitmq_data:/var/lib/rabbitmq
        - ./rabbitmq/definitions.json:/etc/rabbitmq/definitions.json                                                                                                                                                      
        - ./rabbitmq/rabbitmq.conf:/etc/rabbitmq/rabbitmq.conf                                                                                                                                                            
      ports:
        - "5672:5672"                                                                                                                                                                                                     
        - "15672:15672"   # Management UI
        - "61613:61613"   # STOMP plugin                                                                                                                                                                                  
      networks:
        - cinetix-net                                                                                                                                                                                                     
      healthcheck:
        test: ["CMD", "rabbitmq-diagnostics", "ping"]
        interval: 10s                                                                                                                                                                                                     
        timeout: 5s
        retries: 10                                                                                                                                                                                                       
                  
    # ä¤ä¤ Keycloak ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤                                                                                                                                      
    keycloak:
      image: quay.io/keycloak/keycloak:25.0

      environment:                                                                                                                                                                                                        
        KC_DB:               postgres

        KEYCLOAK_ADMIN:      admin

      volumes:

      ports:

          condition: service_healthy                                                                                                                                                                                      
      networks:
        - cinetix-net                                                                                                                                                                                                     
                  
    # ä¤ä¤ MinIO (S3-compatible object storage) ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤

# ä¤ä¤ä¤ Pod Disruption Budget ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤

# ä¤ä¤ä¤ Node affinity ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤

- key:      app

values:   ["booking-service"]

# ä¤ä¤ä¤ Graceful shutdown ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤

templates/deployment.yaml:

# templates/deployment.yaml
apiVersion: apps/v1
kind: Deployment
metadata:
name: {{ include "booking-service.fullname" . }}
labels:                                                                                                                                                                                                               
{{- include "booking-service.labels" . | nindent 4 }}
spec:                                                                                                                                                                                                                   
{{- if not .Values.autoscaling.enabled }}
replicas: {{ .Values.replicaCount }}
{{- end }}                                                                                                                                                                                                            
strategy:
type: RollingUpdate                                                                                                                                                                                                 
rollingUpdate:
maxSurge:       1
maxUnavailable: 0   # Zero-downtime deployment
selector:                                                                                                                                                                                                             
matchLabels:
{{- include "booking-service.selectorLabels" . | nindent 6 }}                                                                                                                                                     
template:     
metadata:                                                                                                                                                                                                           
annotations:
# Force pod restart khi configmap/secret thay ??i                                                                                                                                                               
checksum/config: {{ include (print $.Template.BasePath "/configmap.yaml") . | sha256sum }}
checksum/secret: {{ include (print $.Template.BasePath "/secret.yaml")    . | sha256sum }}                                                                                                                      
{{- with .Values.podAnnotations }}                                                                                                                                                                              
{{- toYaml . | nindent 8 }}                                                                                                                                                                                     
{{- end }}                                                                                                                                                                                                      
labels:   
{{- include "booking-service.selectorLabels" . | nindent 8 }}
version: {{ .Values.image.tag | default .Chart.AppVersion | quote }}                                                                                                                                            
spec:
serviceAccountName: {{ include "booking-service.serviceAccountName" . }}                                                                                                                                          
securityContext:                                                                                                                                                                                                  
{{- toYaml .Values.podSecurityContext | nindent 8 }}
terminationGracePeriodSeconds: {{ .Values.terminationGracePeriodSeconds }}

        containers:
          - name: {{ .Chart.Name }}                                                                                                                                                                                       
            securityContext:
              {{- toYaml .Values.securityContext | nindent 12 }}
            image: "{{ .Values.image.repository }}:{{ .Values.image.tag | default .Chart.AppVersion }}"                                                                                                                   
            imagePullPolicy: {{ .Values.image.pullPolicy }}
            ports:                                                                                                                                                                                                        
              - name: http
                containerPort: 8082

              - name: grpc
                containerPort: 9082                                                                                                                                                                                       
                protocol:      TCP
            envFrom:
              - configMapRef:
                  name: {{ .Values.envFromConfigMap | first }}
              - secretRef:                                                                                                                                                                                                
                  name: {{ .Values.envFromSecret | first }}
            env:                                                                                                                                                                                                          
              {{- range $key, $val := .Values.env }}
              - name:  {{ $key }}                                                                                                                                                                                         
                value: {{ $val | quote }}
              {{- end }}                                                                                                                                                                                                  
              # Pod metadata injection
              - name:  POD_NAME                                                                                                                                                                                           
                valueFrom:
                  fieldRef:                                                                                                                                                                                               
                    fieldPath: metadata.name
              - name:  POD_NAMESPACE
                valueFrom:                                                                                                                                                                                                
                  fieldRef:
                    fieldPath: metadata.namespace                                                                                                                                                                         
              - name:  NODE_NAME
                valueFrom:
                  fieldRef:
                    fieldPath: spec.nodeName
            resources:
              {{- toYaml .Values.resources | nindent 12 }}
            livenessProbe:                                                                                                                                                                                                
              {{- toYaml .Values.livenessProbe | nindent 12 }}
            readinessProbe:                                                                                                                                                                                               
              {{- toYaml .Values.readinessProbe | nindent 12 }}
            startupProbe:                                                                                                                                                                                                 
              {{- toYaml .Values.startupProbe | nindent 12 }}
            lifecycle:                                                                                                                                                                                                    
              {{- toYaml .Values.lifecycle | nindent 12 }}
            volumeMounts:                                                                                                                                                                                                 
              {{- toYaml .Values.extraVolumeMounts | nindent 12 }}
        volumes:                                                                                                                                                                                                          
          {{- toYaml .Values.extraVolumes | nindent 8 }}
        {{- with .Values.nodeSelector }}                                                                                                                                                                                  
        nodeSelector:
          {{- toYaml . | nindent 8 }}                                                                                                                                                                                     
        {{- end }}
        {{- with .Values.affinity }}

          {{- toYaml . | nindent 8 }}
        {{- end }}

PostgreSQL StatefulSet (per-service pattern):

# infrastructure/k8s/infra/postgres/booking-postgres.yaml
apiVersion: apps/v1                                                                                                                                                                                                     
kind: StatefulSet
metadata:                                                                                                                                                                                                               
name:      postgres-booking
namespace: cinetix
spec:                                                                                                                                                                                                                   
serviceName: postgres-booking
replicas: 1    # Primary only ü\ d?ng CloudSQL/RDS n?u c?n HA                                                                                                                                                          
selector:                                                                                                                                                                                                             
matchLabels:
app: postgres-booking                                                                                                                                                                                             
template:                                                                                                                                                                                                             
metadata:
labels:                                                                                                                                                                                                           
app: postgres-booking
spec:
securityContext:
fsGroup: 999
containers:
- name: postgres
image: postgres:16-alpine                                                                                                                                                                                     
env:
- name:  POSTGRES_DB                                                                                                                                                                                        
value: booking_db
- name:  POSTGRES_USER
valueFrom:
secretKeyRef:
name: postgres-booking-secret                                                                                                                                                                         
key:  username
- name:  POSTGRES_PASSWORD                                                                                                                                                                                  
valueFrom:
secretKeyRef:
name: postgres-booking-secret
key:  password                                                                                                                                                                                        
# Debezium c?n WAL level = logical
- name:  POSTGRES_INITDB_ARGS                                                                                                                                                                               
value: "--wal-level=logical"                                                                                                                                                                              
args:
- "-c"                                                                                                                                                                                                      
- "wal_level=logical"
- "-c"
- "max_replication_slots=10"                                                                                                                                                                                
- "-c"
- "max_wal_senders=10"                                                                                                                                                                                      
- "-c"
- "shared_preload_libraries=pg_stat_statements"
ports:                                                                                                                                                                                                        
- containerPort: 5432
resources:                                                                                                                                                                                                    
requests:
cpu:    500m
memory: 1Gi
limits:
cpu:    2000m
memory: 4Gi                                                                                                                                                                                               
volumeMounts:
- name: postgres-data                                                                                                                                                                                       
mountPath: /var/lib/postgresql/data
- name: postgres-config
mountPath: /etc/postgresql/postgresql.conf                                                                                                                                                                
subPath: postgresql.conf
readinessProbe:                                                                                                                                                                                               
exec:
command: ["pg_isready", "-U", "postgres"]
initialDelaySeconds: 5                                                                                                                                                                                      
periodSeconds: 10
livenessProbe:                                                                                                                                                                                                
exec:
command: ["pg_isready", "-U", "postgres"]
initialDelaySeconds: 30
periodSeconds: 15                                                                                                                                                                                           
volumes:
- name: postgres-config                                                                                                                                                                                         
configMap:
name: postgres-booking-config
volumeClaimTemplates:
- metadata:                                                                                                                                                                                                         
name: postgres-data
spec:                                                                                                                                                                                                             
accessModes: ["ReadWriteOnce"]
storageClassName: standard-rwo   # GKE standard; d?ng gp3 tr?n EKS
resources:                                                                                                                                                                                                      
requests:
storage: 20Gi
                  
---
apiVersion: v1
kind: Service
metadata:
name:      postgres-booking
namespace: cinetix
spec:                                                                                                                                                                                                                   
selector:
app: postgres-booking                                                                                                                                                                                               
ports:        
- port:       5432
targetPort: 5432
clusterIP: None   # Headless service cho StatefulSet

RabbitMQ via Operator:

# infrastructure/k8s/infra/rabbitmq/rabbitmq-cluster.yaml
# D?ng RabbitMQ Cluster Operator (khuy?n ngh? h?n t? manage StatefulSet)
apiVersion: rabbitmq.com/v1beta1                                                                                                                                                                                        
kind: RabbitmqCluster                                                                                                                                                                                                   
metadata:                                                                                                                                                                                                               
name:      cinetix-rabbitmq
namespace: cinetix                                                                                                                                                                                                    
spec:           
replicas: 3
image: rabbitmq:3.13-management
resources:                                                                                                                                                                                                            
requests:
cpu:    500m                                                                                                                                                                                                      
memory: 1Gi
limits:
cpu:    2000m
memory: 2Gi
rabbitmq:                                                                                                                                                                                                             
additionalPlugins:
- rabbitmq_management                                                                                                                                                                                             
- rabbitmq_prometheus
- rabbitmq_shovel
- rabbitmq_stomp          # Cho WebSocket STOMP                                                                                                                                                                   
additionalConfig: |
default_vhost = /cinetix                                                                                                                                                                                          
# Message persistence
vm_memory_high_watermark.relative = 0.7                                                                                                                                                                           
# DLQ configuration
dead_letter_exchange = cinetix.dlx                                                                                                                                                                                
persistence:                                                                                                                                                                                                          
storageClassName: standard-rwo
storage:          10Gi                                                                                                                                                                                              
affinity:                                                                                                                                                                                                             
podAntiAffinity:
requiredDuringSchedulingIgnoredDuringExecution:                                                                                                                                                                   
- labelSelector:
matchLabels:
app.kubernetes.io/name: cinetix-rabbitmq                                                                                                                                                                  
topologyKey: kubernetes.io/hostname
                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
---             
# RabbitMQ exchanges, queues, bindings (via definition import)
apiVersion: rabbitmq.com/v1beta1                                                                                                                                                                                        
kind: Exchange                                                                                                                                                                                                          
metadata:                                                                                                                                                                                                               
name:      cinetix-events                                                                                                                                                                                             
namespace: cinetix
spec:
name:       cinetix.events
type:       topic
durable:    true
rabbitmqClusterReference:                                                                                                                                                                                             
name: cinetix-rabbitmq
                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
---             
apiVersion: rabbitmq.com/v1beta1
kind: Queue
metadata:
name:      booking-payment-events
namespace: cinetix                                                                                                                                                                                                    
spec:
name:    booking-svc.payment.events                                                                                                                                                                                   
durable: true                                                                                                                                                                                                         
arguments:
x-dead-letter-exchange:    cinetix.dlx                                                                                                                                                                              
x-dead-letter-routing-key: booking-svc.payment.events.dlq
x-message-ttl:             1800000   # 30 ph?t                                                                                                                                                                      
rabbitmqClusterReference:
name: cinetix-rabbitmq
                  
---                                                                                                                                                                                                                     
apiVersion: rabbitmq.com/v1beta1
kind: Binding
metadata:
name:      booking-payment-binding
namespace: cinetix                                                                                                                                                                                                    
spec:
source:          cinetix.events                                                                                                                                                                                       
destination:     booking-svc.payment.events
destinationType: queue
routingKey:      "payment.events.#"
rabbitmqClusterReference:                                                                                                                                                                                             
name: cinetix-rabbitmq
