7.5 GitHub Actions CI/CD

ci.yml ü\ Build, Test, Scan:

# .github/workflows/ci.yml
name: CI Pipeline

on:                                                                                                                                                                                                                     
push:         
branches: [main, develop, "feature/**", "fix/**"]
pull_request:
branches: [main, develop]

env:
JAVA_VERSION: "21"                                                                                                                                                                                                    
REGISTRY:     ghcr.io
IMAGE_PREFIX: ghcr.io/${{ github.repository_owner }}/cinetix

jobs:
# ä¤ä¤ä¤ Detect changed services ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤                                                                                                                                         
detect-changes:                                                                                                                                                                                                       
runs-on: ubuntu-latest
outputs:                                                                                                                                                                                                            
services: ${{ steps.filter.outputs.services }}
matrix:   ${{ steps.set-matrix.outputs.matrix }}                                                                                                                                                                  
steps:
- uses: actions/checkout@v4                                                                                                                                                                                       
- uses: dorny/paths-filter@v3                                                                                                                                                                                     
id: filter
with:                                                                                                                                                                                                           
filters: |
booking-service:
- 'services/booking-service/**'
- 'libs/**'                                                                                                                                                                                               
showtime-service:
- 'services/showtime-service/**'                                                                                                                                                                          
- 'libs/**'
payment-service:                                                                                                                                                                                            
- 'services/payment-service/**'
- 'libs/**'                                                                                                                                                                                               
# ... other services

        - id: set-matrix
          run: |
            SERVICES=()                                                                                                                                                                                                   
            if [[ "${{ steps.filter.outputs.booking-service }}" == "true" ]]; then
              SERVICES+=("booking-service")                                                                                                                                                                               
            fi                                                                                                                                                                                                            
            if [[ "${{ steps.filter.outputs.showtime-service }}" == "true" ]]; then
              SERVICES+=("showtime-service")                                                                                                                                                                              
            fi    
            if [ ${#SERVICES[@]} -eq 0 ]; then
              SERVICES+=("none")                                                                                                                                                                                          
            fi
            echo "matrix=$(printf '%s\n' "${SERVICES[@]}" | jq -R . | jq -sc .)" \                                                                                                                                        
              >> $GITHUB_OUTPUT                                                                                                                                                                                           
   
    # ä¤ä¤ä¤ Build & Unit Test ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤                                                                                                                                         
    build-and-test:                                                                                                                                                                                                       
      needs: detect-changes
      if: ${{ needs.detect-changes.outputs.matrix != '["none"]' }}                                                                                                                                                        
      runs-on: ubuntu-latest                                                                                                                                                                                              
      strategy:
        matrix:                                                                                                                                                                                                           
          service: ${{ fromJson(needs.detect-changes.outputs.matrix) }}
        fail-fast: false                                                                                                                                                                                                  
   
      steps:                                                                                                                                                                                                              
        - uses: actions/checkout@v4

        - uses: actions/setup-java@v4
          with:
            java-version:     ${{ env.JAVA_VERSION }}                                                                                                                                                                     
            distribution:     temurin
            cache:            maven                                                                                                                                                                                       
                  
        - name: Build & Unit Test
          run: |
            ./mvnw test \
              -pl services/${{ matrix.service }} -am \                                                                                                                                                                    
              --no-transfer-progress \
              -Dspring.profiles.active=test                                                                                                                                                                               
                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
        - name: Upload coverage to Codecov
          uses: codecov/codecov-action@v4                                                                                                                                                                                 
          with:                                                                                                                                                                                                           
            file: services/${{ matrix.service }}/target/site/jacoco/jacoco.xml
            flags: ${{ matrix.service }}                                                                                                                                                                                  
                  
    # ä¤ä¤ä¤ Integration Tests (Testcontainers) ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤                                                                                                                                         
    integration-test:
      needs: build-and-test                                                                                                                                                                                               
      runs-on: ubuntu-latest                                                                                                                                                                                              
      strategy:
        matrix:                                                                                                                                                                                                           
          service: ${{ fromJson(needs.detect-changes.outputs.matrix) }}

      services:                                                                                                                                                                                                           
        # Testcontainers t? qu?n l? containers ü\ kh?ng c?n service definitions ? ??y
        # Ch? c?n Docker socket access                                                                                                                                                                                    
                  
      steps:                                                                                                                                                                                                              
        - uses: actions/checkout@v4
        - uses: actions/setup-java@v4
          with:
            java-version:  ${{ env.JAVA_VERSION }}                                                                                                                                                                        
            distribution:  temurin
            cache:         maven                                                                                                                                                                                          
                  
        - name: Integration Tests
          run: |
            ./mvnw verify \
              -pl services/${{ matrix.service }} -am \                                                                                                                                                                    
              --no-transfer-progress \
              -P integration-test \                                                                                                                                                                                       
              -Dspring.profiles.active=test
          env:                                                                                                                                                                                                            
            TESTCONTAINERS_RYUK_DISABLED: true
                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
    # ä¤ä¤ä¤ SAST ü\ SonarQube ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤                                                                                                                                         
    sast:
      needs: build-and-test                                                                                                                                                                                               
      runs-on: ubuntu-latest
      if: github.event_name == 'pull_request'
      steps:                                                                                                                                                                                                              
        - uses: actions/checkout@v4
          with:                                                                                                                                                                                                           
            fetch-depth: 0   # SonarQube c?n full history
                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
        - uses: actions/setup-java@v4
          with:                                                                                                                                                                                                           
            java-version: ${{ env.JAVA_VERSION }}
            distribution: temurin
            cache:         maven
                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
        - name: SonarQube Scan
          run: |                                                                                                                                                                                                          
            ./mvnw sonar:sonar \
              --no-transfer-progress \
              -Dsonar.host.url=${{ secrets.SONAR_URL }} \
              -Dsonar.login=${{ secrets.SONAR_TOKEN }} \                                                                                                                                                                  
              -Dsonar.pullrequest.key=${{ github.event.pull_request.number }} \
              -Dsonar.pullrequest.branch=${{ github.head_ref }} \                                                                                                                                                         
              -Dsonar.pullrequest.base=${{ github.base_ref }}
                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
    # ä¤ä¤ä¤ Build Docker Images ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤ä¤
    docker-build:                                                                                                                                                                                                         
      needs: [build-and-test, integration-test]
      runs-on: ubuntu-latest                                                                                                                                                                                              
      if: github.ref == 'refs/heads/main' || github.ref == 'refs/heads/develop'
      strategy:                                                                                                                                                                                                           
        matrix:   
          service: ${{ fromJson(needs.detect-changes.outputs.matrix) }}
                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
      permissions:
        contents: read                                                                                                                                                                                                    
        packages: write

      steps:
        - uses: actions/checkout@v4

        - uses: docker/setup-buildx-action@v3                                                                                                                                                                             
   
        - uses: docker/login-action@v3                                                                                                                                                                                    
          with:   
            registry: ${{ env.REGISTRY }}
            username: ${{ github.actor }}
            password: ${{ secrets.GITHUB_TOKEN }}
                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
        - name: Docker meta
          id: meta                                                                                                                                                                                                        
          uses: docker/metadata-action@v5
          with:
            images: ${{ env.IMAGE_PREFIX }}/${{ matrix.service }}
            tags: |                                                                                                                                                                                                       
              type=sha,prefix=sha-,format=short
              type=ref,event=branch                                                                                                                                                                                       
              type=raw,value=latest,enable=${{ github.ref == 'refs/heads/main' }}                                                                                                                                         
   
        - name: Build & Push                                                                                                                                                                                              
          uses: docker/build-push-action@v6
          with:
            context:   .
            file:      services/${{ matrix.service }}/Dockerfile                                                                                                                                                          
            push:      true
            tags:      ${{ steps.meta.outputs.tags }}                                                                                                                                                                     
            labels:    ${{ steps.meta.outputs.labels }}
            cache-from: type=gha,scope=${{ matrix.service }}
            cache-to:   type=gha,scope=${{ matrix.service }},mode=max                                                                                                                                                     
            build-args: |
              BUILD_DATE=${{ github.event.head_commit.timestamp }}                                                                                                                                                        
              GIT_COMMIT=${{ github.sha }}                                                                                                                                                                                
   
        - name: Container Security Scan (Trivy)                                                                                                                                                                           
          uses: aquasecurity/trivy-action@master                                                                                                                                                                          
          with:
            image-ref: ${{ env.IMAGE_PREFIX }}/${{ matrix.service }}:sha-${{ github.sha }}                                                                                                                                
            format:    sarif                                                                                                                                                                                              
            output:    trivy-results.sarif
            severity:  CRITICAL,HIGH                                                                                                                                                                                      
            exit-code: 1   # Fail CI n?u c? CRITICAL vulnerability
                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
        - name: Upload Trivy results
          uses: github/codeql-action/upload-sarif@v3                                                                                                                                                                      
          with:                                                                                                                                                                                                           
            sarif_file: trivy-results.sarif

release.yml ü\ Tag Release + Bump Chart Version:

# .github/workflows/release.yml
name: Release

on:
push:
tags:
- "v*.*.*"   # Semantic versioning: v1.2.3

env:
REGISTRY:     ghcr.io                                                                                                                                                                                                 
IMAGE_PREFIX: ghcr.io/${{ github.repository_owner }}/cinetix

jobs:
release:                                                                                                                                                                                                              
runs-on: ubuntu-latest
permissions:
contents: write
packages: write

      steps:                                                                                                                                                                                                              
        - uses: actions/checkout@v4
          with:                                                                                                                                                                                                           
            fetch-depth: 0

        - name: Extract version
          id: version
          run: echo "VERSION=${GITHUB_REF#refs/tags/v}" >> $GITHUB_OUTPUT
                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
        - uses: docker/setup-buildx-action@v3
        - uses: docker/login-action@v3                                                                                                                                                                                    
          with:                                                                                                                                                                                                           
            registry: ${{ env.REGISTRY }}
            username: ${{ github.actor }}                                                                                                                                                                                 
            password: ${{ secrets.GITHUB_TOKEN }}

        # Build & push t?t c? services v?i version tag                                                                                                                                                                    
        - name: Build & Push All Services
          run: |                                                                                                                                                                                                          
            SERVICES=(
              booking-service showtime-service movie-service                                                                                                                                                              
              cinema-service payment-service ticket-service
              promotion-service notification-service chat-service                                                                                                                                                         
              api-gateway identity-service                                                                                                                                                                                
            )
            for SERVICE in "${SERVICES[@]}"; do                                                                                                                                                                           
              docker buildx build \
                --platform linux/amd64,linux/arm64 \                                                                                                                                                                      
                -f services/$SERVICE/Dockerfile \
                -t "${{ env.IMAGE_PREFIX }}/$SERVICE:${{ steps.version.outputs.VERSION }}" \                                                                                                                              
                -t "${{ env.IMAGE_PREFIX }}/$SERVICE:latest" \                                                                                                                                                            
                --push \
                --cache-from type=gha,scope=$SERVICE \                                                                                                                                                                    
                .                                                                                                                                                                                                         
            done
                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
        # Update Helm chart versions (GitOps)
        - name: Bump Helm Chart Versions                                                                                                                                                                                  
          run: |
            VERSION=${{ steps.version.outputs.VERSION }}                                                                                                                                                                  
            for CHART in infrastructure/helm/charts/*/; do
              SERVICE=$(basename $CHART)                                                                                                                                                                                  
              # Update appVersion trong Chart.yaml
              sed -i "s/^appVersion:.*/appVersion: \"${VERSION}\"/" $CHART/Chart.yaml                                                                                                                                     
              # Update image tag trong values.yaml                                                                                                                                                                        
              sed -i "s/^  tag:.*/  tag: \"${VERSION}\"/" $CHART/values.yaml
            done                                                                                                                                                                                                          
                  
        - name: Commit Chart Updates                                                                                                                                                                                      
          uses: stefanzweifel/git-auto-commit-action@v5                                                                                                                                                                   
          with:
            commit_message: "chore: bump chart versions to ${{ steps.version.outputs.VERSION }}"                                                                                                                          
            branch:         main                                                                                                                                                                                          
            file_pattern:   "infrastructure/helm/**"
                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
        # Generate Release Notes t? Conventional Commits                                                                                                                                                                  
        - name: Generate Release Notes
          id: release-notes                                                                                                                                                                                               
          uses: orhun/git-cliff-action@v3
          with:                                                                                                                                                                                                           
            config: cliff.toml
            args:   --current --strip header                                                                                                                                                                              
                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
        - name: Create GitHub Release
          uses: softprops/action-gh-release@v2                                                                                                                                                                            
          with:                                                                                                                                                                                                           
            body:      ${{ steps.release-notes.outputs.content }}
            draft:     false                                                                                                                                                                                              
            prerelease: ${{ contains(github.ref, '-rc') || contains(github.ref, '-beta') }}

ArgoCD ApplicationSet:

# infrastructure/k8s/argocd/applicationset.yaml
apiVersion: argoproj.io/v1alpha1
kind: ApplicationSet
metadata:
name:      cinetix-services                                                                                                                                                                                           
namespace: argocd
spec:                                                                                                                                                                                                                   
generators:   
- list:
elements:
- service:     booking-service
namespace:   cinetix                                                                                                                                                                                        
environment: production
- service:     showtime-service                                                                                                                                                                               
namespace:   cinetix
environment: production
- service:     payment-service
namespace:   cinetix                                                                                                                                                                                        
environment: production
- service:     movie-service                                                                                                                                                                                  
namespace:   cinetix
environment: production
- service:     cinema-service
namespace:   cinetix
environment: production
- service:     ticket-service
namespace:   cinetix                                                                                                                                                                                        
environment: production
- service:     promotion-service                                                                                                                                                                              
namespace:   cinetix
environment: production
- service:     notification-service
namespace:   cinetix
environment: production
- service:     chat-service                                                                                                                                                                                   
namespace:   cinetix
environment: production                                                                                                                                                                                     
- service:     api-gateway
namespace:   cinetix
environment: production
- service:     identity-service
namespace:   cinetix
environment: production

    template:
      metadata:                                                                                                                                                                                                           
        name: "cinetix-{{service}}"
        labels:
          environment: "{{environment}}"
        annotations:                                                                                                                                                                                                      
          # Slack notification khi sync
          notifications.argoproj.io/subscribe.on-sync-succeeded.slack: cinetix-deploys                                                                                                                                    
          notifications.argoproj.io/subscribe.on-sync-failed.slack:    cinetix-alerts                                                                                                                                     
      spec:                                                                                                                                                                                                               
        project: cinetix                                                                                                                                                                                                  
                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
        source:
          repoURL:        https://github.com/your-org/cinetix                                                                                                                                                             
          targetRevision: main
          path:           infrastructure/helm/charts/{{service}}
          helm:                                                                                                                                                                                                           
            releaseName: "{{service}}"
            valueFiles:                                                                                                                                                                                                   
              - values.yaml
              - values-production.yaml                                                                                                                                                                                    
            # Secrets inject t? Vault (External Secrets)
            # Kh?ng hardcode secrets trong Git                                                                                                                                                                            
                  
        destination:                                                                                                                                                                                                      
          server:    https://kubernetes.default.svc
          namespace: "{{namespace}}"
                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
        syncPolicy:
          automated:                                                                                                                                                                                                      
            prune:    true    # X?a resources kh?ng c?n trong Git
            selfHeal: true    # Auto-revert manual changes                                                                                                                                                                
          syncOptions:
            - CreateNamespace=true                                                                                                                                                                                        
            - PrunePropagationPolicy=foreground
            - RespectIgnoreDifferences=true                                                                                                                                                                               
          retry:
            limit: 3                                                                                                                                                                                                      
            backoff:
              duration:    5s
              factor:      2                                                                                                                                                                                              
              maxDuration: 3m
                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
        # Ignore HPA replicas (managed by HPA, kh?ng c?n sync)                                                                                                                                                            
        ignoreDifferences:
          - group:       apps                                                                                                                                                                                             
            kind:        Deployment
            jsonPointers:                                                                                                                                                                                                 
              - /spec/replicas
          - group:       autoscaling                                                                                                                                                                                      
            kind:        HorizontalPodAutoscaler
            jsonPointers:
              - /spec/metrics

  ---                                                                                                                                                                                                                     
# ArgoCD Project v?i RBAC

- namespace: monitoring
server:    https://kubernetes.default.svc
clusterResourceWhitelist:
- group: ""                                                                                                                                                                                                         
kind:  Namespace
namespaceResourceWhitelist:                                                                                                                                                                                           
- group: "*"
kind:  "*"

description: Read-only access
policies:                                                                                                                                                                                                         
- p, proj:cinetix:developer, applications, get, cinetix/*, allow
- p, proj:cinetix:developer, applications, sync, cinetix/*, deny                                                                                                                                                
- name:        deployer                                                                                                                                                                                             
description: Can sync applications                                                                                                                                                                                
policies:                                                                                                                                                                                                         
- p, proj:cinetix:deployer, applications, *, cinetix/*, allow

cliff.toml ü\ Conventional Commits Release Notes:

# cliff.toml
[changelog]     
header = """
# Changelog\n
All notable changes to CinemaTix.\n
"""
body = """                                                                                                                                                                                                              
{% if version %}\
## [{{ version | trim_start_matches(pat="v") }}] - {{ timestamp | date(format="%Y-%m-%d") }}
{% else %}\
## [Unreleased]
{% endif %}\                                                                                                                                                                                                            
{% for group, commits in commits | group_by(attribute="group") %}
### {{ group | striptags | trim | upper_first }}
{% for commit in commits %}
- {% if commit.scope %}**{{ commit.scope }}**: {% endif %}{{ commit.message }}\
  {% endfor %}                                                                                                                                                                                                            
  {% endfor %}\n  
  """

[git]
conventional_commits = true
commit_parsers = [
{ message = "^feat",     group = "Features" },                                                                                                                                                                        
{ message = "^fix",      group = "Bug Fixes" },                                                                                                                                                                       
{ message = "^perf",     group = "Performance" },                                                                                                                                                                     
{ message = "^refactor", group = "Refactoring" },                                                                                                                                                                     
{ message = "^chore",    group = "Miscellaneous", skip = true },
]                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
filter_commits = true
tag_pattern    = "v[0-9]*"
                  
---                                                                                                                                                                                                                     
?? Nh?ng ?i?m b?n c?n l?u ?:

1. Zero-downtime deployment v?i RollingUpdate:
   maxUnavailable: 0  ü© Kh?ng bao gi? c? pod unavailable trong qu? tr?nh deploy                                                                                                                                            
   maxSurge: 1        ü© T?o 1 pod m?i tr??c khi terminate pod c?               
   preStop sleep 10s  ü© Cho load balancer drain connections tr??c khi terminate                                                                                                                                            
   terminationGracePeriod: 60s ü© Spring Boot 60s ?? finish in-flight requests

2. Secret Management ü\ Kh?ng commit secrets v?o Git:                                                                                                                                                                    
   Option 1: External Secrets Operator + AWS Secrets Manager                                                                                                                                                               
   ü© ESO t? sync secrets t? AWS v?o K8s Secret objects

Option 2: HashiCorp Vault + Vault Agent Injector                                                                                                                                                                        
ü© Vault sidecar inject secrets v?o pod filesystem

Option 3: Sealed Secrets (Bitnami)                                                                                                                                                                                      
ü© Encrypt secrets b?ng cluster public key, safe to commit

Khuy?n ngh?: External Secrets Operator cho GKE/EKS (native cloud integration)

3. Database Migration trong K8s:                                                                                                                                                                                        
   D?ng Flyway migrate ch?y nh? Init Container tr??c khi app start:

initContainers:                                                                                                                                                                                                         
- name: flyway-migrate
image: flyway/flyway:10-alpine                                                                                                                                                                                      
command: ["flyway", "migrate"]
env:                          
- name: FLYWAY_URL                                                                                                                                                                                                
value: jdbc:postgresql://postgres-booking:5432/booking_db
# ??m b?o migration ho?n th?nh tr??c khi main container start

4. Multi-arch image (Apple Silicon M1/M2 dev):                                                                                                                                                                          
   --platform linux/amd64,linux/arm64                                                                                                                                                                                      
   Docker buildx t?o manifest list ü\ c?ng 1 tag ch?y tr?n c? x86 v? ARM.                                                                                                                                                   
   Quan tr?ng n?u team dev d?ng Mac M1/M2.
